
namespace = flavor_feiten

######################################
# State sponsored whaling expedition #
######################################

# Set off
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.1
	title = flavor_feiten.1.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.1.desc
	picture = WOKOU_INCIDENT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_active_whaling_expedition
				duration = -1
			}
			set_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition
		}
	}

	# Letsago
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.1.a
		tooltip = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_active_whaling_expedition
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.2 days = 180 random = 60 } }
	}
}

# Bored at sea
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.2
	title = flavor_feiten.2.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.2.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition }

	# Adm (its candle wax/lantern oil)
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.2.a
		set_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_adm
		custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.2.tt
		add_adm_power = -50
	}
	# Dip (its Ambergris)
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.2.b
		set_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_dip
		custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.2.tt
		add_dip_power = -50
	}
	# Mil (its baleen and its myriad uses)
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.2.c
		set_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_mil
		custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.2.tt
		add_mil_power = -50
	}
	# We got no time to waste on these friviolities
	option = { name = flavor_feiten.2.d }
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_feiten.3
				days = 120 random = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

# The hunt begins
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.3
	title = flavor_feiten.3.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.3.desc
	picture = JANISSARIES_IN_FORMATION_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition }

	# Volunteer for one of the boats
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.3.a
		add_republican_tradition_excess_to_mana_effect = { VAL = 5 }
		add_prestige_excess_to_splendour_effect = { VAL = 5 }
		random_list = {
			# Injured
			50 = {
				custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.3.injuredtt
				set_country_flag = feiten_injured_by_whale
			}
			# You're fine
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					mil = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					mil = 6
				}
				set_country_flag = feiten_whale_slayed
			}
		}
	}
	# Sit back and watch... carefully
	option = { name = flavor_feiten.3.b }

	after = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.4 } }
}

# Hunt results
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.4
	title = flavor_feiten.4.title
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_injured_by_whale }
		desc = flavor_feiten.4.descInjured
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_slayed }
		desc = flavor_feiten.4.descMobyDicked # No I haven't read the book :P
	}
	desc = flavor_feiten.4.satBack
	
	picture = GREAT_MAN_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition }

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.4.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_slayed }
			add_prestige_or_monarch_power = { amount = 25 }
			add_ruler_modifier = { name = feiten_whale_slayer duration = -1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = feiten_injured_by_whale }
			add_ruler_modifier = { name = feiten_whaling_injury duration = -1 }
		}
	}

	after = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.5 days = 120 random = 30 } }
}

# Bored at sea redux
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.5
	title = flavor_feiten.5.title
	desc = {
		desc = flavor_feiten.5.desc.oil
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_adm }
	}
	desc = {
		desc = flavor_feiten.5.desc.ambergis
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_dip }
	}
	desc = {
		desc = flavor_feiten.5.desc.baleen
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_mil }
	}
	desc = flavor_feiten.5.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition }

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.5.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_adm }
		change_adm = 1
		4878 = { # 
			change_trade_goods = naval_supplies
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_lantern_oil
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.5.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_dip }
		change_dip = 1
		4878 = {
			change_trade_goods = incense
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_ambergris
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.5.c
		trigger = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_mil }
		change_mil = 1
		4878 = {
			change_trade_goods = ivory
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_baleen
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.5.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_mil }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_dip }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_adm }
		}
		4878 = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_whale_meat
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	after = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.6 days = 60 random = 10 } }
}

# Triumphant return
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.6
	title = flavor_feiten.6.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.6.desc
	picture = HARBOUR_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition }

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.6.a
		remove_country_modifier = feiten_active_whaling_expedition
		clr_ruler_flag = feiten_on_whaling_expedition
		clr_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_mil
		clr_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_dip
		clr_country_flag = feiten_whale_expedition_adm
		clr_country_flag = feiten_whale_slayed
		clr_country_flag = feiten_injured_by_whale
	}
}

# Our guy dies during the trip

		name = flavor_feiten.7.a
		remove_country_modifier = feiten_active_whaling_expedition
	}
}

# Intro/start
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.30
	title = flavor_feiten.30.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.30.desc
	picture = east_asian_ADVISOR_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Favor Xiao Yang's theory and research
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.30.a
		set_country_flag = xiao_yang_favored
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_church
			loyalty = 10
		}
	}

	# Favor Da Jin's theory and research
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.30.b
		set_country_flag = da_jin_favored
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_eunuchs_anb
			loyalty = 10
		}
	}

	after = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.31 days = 1095 random = 180 } } }
}

# Struggles
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.31
	title = flavor_feiten.31.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.31.desc
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes


	# Delays? Keep at it champ
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.31.a
		country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.32 days = 1825 random = 365 }
	}

	# Moar powah!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.31.b
		add_dip_power = -25
		add_mil_power = -25
		add_adm_power = -25
		country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.32 days = 365 random = 90 }
	}

	# Have them work together
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.31.c
		trigger = {
			employed_advisor = {
				category = ADM
				is_male = no
				type = natural_scientist
			}
			natural_scientist = 2
			employed_advisor = {
				category = MIL
				is_male = yes
				type = fortification_expert
			}
			fortification_expert = 2
		}
		add_republican_tradition_excess_to_mana_effect = { VAL = 10 }
		country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.32 days = 365 random = 90 }
		clr_country_flag = da_jin_favored
		clr_country_flag = xiao_yang_favored
		set_country_flag = balloon_research_teamwork
	}
}

# Prototype complete!
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.32
	title = flavor_feiten.32.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.32.desc
	picture = BIG_STAR_IN_SKY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.32.a
		remove_country_modifier = feiten_starting_balloon_research
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = balloon_research_teamwork }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_teamwork_success
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = da_jin_favored }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_da_jin_success
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = xiao_yang_favored }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_xiao_yang_success
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
	}
}

# The rise and decline of whale hunting #

# Development of 'group' fishing
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.40
	title = flavor_feiten.40.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.40.desc
	picture = BARBARY_PIRATES_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Hell yeah brother
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.40.a
		4878 = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_lantern_oil }
				remove_province_modifier = feiten_lantern_oil
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_lantern_oil_upgraded
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_ambergris }
				remove_province_modifier = feiten_ambergris
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_ambergris_upgraded
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_baleen }
				remove_province_modifier = feiten_baleen
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_baleen_upgraded
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_whale_meat }
				remove_province_modifier = feiten_whale_meat
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_whale_meat_upgraded
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Collapse of fisheries
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.41
	title = flavor_feiten.41.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.41.desc
	picture = SAD_MERCHANT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Just... tell them to chill for a bit
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.41.a
		4878 = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_fishery_collapse
				duration = 7300
			}
			set_province_flag = feiten_fishery_collapse_no_action
		}
		6147 = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_fishery_collapse
				duration = 7300
			}
			set_province_flag = feiten_fishery_collapse_no_action
		}
		6512 = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_fishery_collapse
				duration = 7300
			}
			set_province_flag = feiten_fishery_collapse_no_action
		}
		add_years_of_income = 1
	}

	# Commission a commitee to figure out what to do/plan better
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.41.b
		4878 = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_fishery_collapse
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
		add_adm_power = -50
	}
}

# Development of modern harpoon guns and steamboats
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.42
	title = flavor_feiten.42.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.42.desc
	picture = TRIBUTARY_FLEET_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# We should pump the brakes a bit
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.42.a
		4878 = { add_base_production = 2 }
		6147 = { add_base_production = 1 }
		6512 = { add_base_production = 1 }
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_artificers
			loyalty = -10
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.43 days = 7300 random = 1825 } }
	}

	# Full steam ahead!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.42.b
		4878 = { add_base_production = 5 }
		6147 = { add_base_production = 2 }
		6512 = { add_base_production = 2 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.43 days = 1825 random = 365 } }
	}
}

# Advocates of the traditional methods get angry
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.43
	title = flavor_feiten.43.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.43.desc
	picture = MERCHANTS_ARGUING_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Give in to their demands
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.43.a
		add_republican_tradition_excess_to_mana_effect = { VAL = 10 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.44 days = 18250 random = 3650 } }
	}

	# The future is now, old man!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.43.b
		add_yearly_sailors = -2
		4878 = { add_unrest = 20 }
		6147 = { add_unrest = 20 }
		6512 = { add_unrest = 20 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.44 days = 7300 random = 1825 } }
	}
}

# Collapse redux
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.44
	title = flavor_feiten.44.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.44.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Oof
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.44.a

			if = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = feiten_fishery_collapse_no_action }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_fishery_collapse_drastic
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_fishery_collapse
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		6147 = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = feiten_fishery_collapse_no_action }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_fishery_collapse_drastic
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_fishery_collapse
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		6512 = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = feiten_fishery_collapse_no_action }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_fishery_collapse_drastic

			else = {

					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# The pirate hunt #
###################
# Strategy
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.50
	title = flavor_feiten.50.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.50.desc
	picture = PIRATE_CAPTAINS_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Lead them into our naval batteries and balloons
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.50.a
		country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.51 }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.3
					has_leader_with = {
						admiral = yes
						fire = 6
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					has_leader_with = {
						admiral = yes
						fire = 5
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					has_leader_with = {
						admiral = yes
						fire = 4
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = feiten_pirate_battle_battery_success
				custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.50.ambushSuccesstt
			}
			1 = {
				custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.50.ambushFailtt
				set_country_flag = feiten_pirate_battle_battery_failure
			}
		}
	}

	# Lay a trap in deep water so our Diokzatgun can fuck em' up
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.50.b
		country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.51 }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.3
					has_leader_with = {
						admiral = yes
						manuever = 6
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					has_leader_with = {
						admiral = yes
						manuever = 5
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					has_leader_with = {
						admiral = yes
						manuever = 4
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.50.ambushSuccesstt
				set_country_flag = feiten_pirate_battle_diokzatgun_success
			}
			1 = {
				custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.50.ambushFailtt
				set_country_flag = feiten_pirate_battle_diokzatgun_failure }
		}
	}
}

# The dread fleet arrives - and its fucking massive
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.51
	title = flavor_feiten.51.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.51.desc
	picture = FLAGSHIP_SUNK_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			1624 = { # Ringlet Basin
				# create_pirate, much like rebels, is scaled off of development(?) so its repeated here a bunch of times to make sure there are enough regardless
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				create_pirate = 6969
				while = {
					limit = { PIR = { num_of_light_ship = 50 } }
					kill_units = {
						who = PIR
						amount = 1
						type = light_ship
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = feiten_pirate_battle_battery_success }
				ringlet_isles_region = {
					limit = {
						country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT
						OR = {
							has_building = naval_battery
							has_building = coastal_defence
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_building = naval_battery }
						1624 = {
							if = {
								limit = { PIR = { num_of_light_ship = 20 } }
								kill_units = {
									who = PIR
									amount = 3
									type = light_ship
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						1624 = {
							if = {
								limit = { PIR = { num_of_light_ship = 30 } }
								kill_units = {
									who = PIR

				}

					type = philosopher
					culture = anbenncoster

					cost_multiplier = 0.25

# Yanshen hates you branch
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.70
	title = flavor_feiten.70.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.70.desc
	picture = BURNING_CITY_ANIMATED_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.70.a
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_bombs_over_tianlou_mod
			duration = 1825
		}
		4871 = {
			change_siege = 10
			add_devastation = 50
			add_base_tax = -2
			add_base_production = -2
			add_base_manpower = -2
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = damaged_temple_complex
					duration = -1
				}
				downgrade_temple_wards = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = derelict_temple_complex
					duration = -1
				}
				downgrade_temple_wards = yes
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			# Savior against the Command
			if = {
				limit = {
					R62 = {
						OR = {
							num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
								value = 20
								superregion = yanshen_superregion
							}
							4826 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = feiten_shift_savior_of_yanshen
				country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.77 days = 365 random = 90 }
			}			
			# Yanshen healthy, they more worried about you
			else = {
				set_country_flag = feiten_shift_accord_of_yanshen
				country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.71 days = 365 random = 90 }
				country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.72 days = 730 random = 180 }
				country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.73 days = 1095 random = 270 }
				country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.75 days = 1825 random = 730 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Someone tries to steal airship tech...
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.71
	title = flavor_feiten.71.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.71.desc
	picture = SPY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_known_country = {
				save_event_target_as = feiten_try_steal_tech_country
			}
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { capital_scope = { superregion = yanshen_superregion } }
				save_event_target_as = feiten_try_steal_tech_country
			}
			random_known_country = {
				limit = {
					ai_attitude = {
						who = ROOT
						attitude = attitude_hostile
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = feiten_try_steal_tech_country
			}
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { is_rival = ROOT }
				save_event_target_as = feiten_try_steal_tech_country
			}
			random_known_country = {
				limit = {
					is_rival = ROOT
					capital_scope = { superregion = yanshen_superregion }
				}
				save_event_target_as = feiten_try_steal_tech_country
			}
		}
	}

	# Kill the man
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.71.a
		event_target:feiten_try_steal_tech_country = {
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = feiten_spy_executed
			}
		}
		add_prestige_excess_to_splendour_effect = { VAL = 5 }
	}

	# Agree with demands and turn the man back over
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.71.b
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
	}
}

			duration = 7300
		}
	}

	# Promise to step back for a bit

			limit = {
				event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target = {

						which = feiten_province_balance
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_nonviolence_max
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feiten_province_balance
						value = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_nonviolence_50
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feiten_province_balance
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_nonviolence_0
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_nonviolence_below
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_artificers
			loyalty = 10
		}
	}
}

# Accord of Yanshen
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.75
	title = flavor_feiten.75.title
	picture = BIG_BOOK_eventPicture
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_shift_accord_of_yanshen }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_shift_savior_of_yanshen }
		}
		desc = flavor_feiten.75.descNoBombsOverTianlou
	}
	desc = flavor_feiten.75.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# We will abide by these terms
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.75.a
		# Gain trade power in Yanshen nodes
		4952 = { # Bianfang
			add_trade_modifier = {
				who = ROOT
				duration = -1
				power = 30
				key = "Accord of Yanshen"
			}
		}
		4859 = { # Yanzhong
			add_trade_modifier = {
				who = ROOT
				duration = -1
				power = 30
				key = "Accord of Yanshen"
			}
		}
		4871 = { # Tianlou
			add_trade_modifier = {
				who = ROOT
				duration = -1
				power = 30
				key = "Accord of Yanshen"
			}
		}
		1371 = { # Feiten
			add_trade_modifier = {
				who = ROOT
				duration = -1
				power = 30
				key = "Accord of Yanshen"
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_shift_accord_of_yanshen }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_shift_savior_of_yanshen }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_accepted_peaceful_accord_of_yanshen
				duration = 18250
			}
			custom_tooltip =  flavor_feiten.75.acceptRestOfYanshenModifiertt1
			tooltip = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = feiten_accepted_peaceful_accord_of_yanshen_rest_of_yanshen
					duration = 18250
				}
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = { superregion = yanshen_superregion }
					NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_monstrous_horde = yes }
				}
				custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.75.acceptRestOfYanshenModifiertt2
				hidden_effect = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = feiten_accepted_peaceful_accord_of_yanshen_rest_of_yanshen
						duration = 18250
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = feiten_resolved_accord_of_yanshen_peaceably
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_accepted_accord_of_yanshen
				duration = 18250
			}
		}
	}

	# We will NOT abide by these terms
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.75.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_shift_accord_of_yanshen }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = feiten_shift_savior_of_yanshen }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_refused_peaceful_accord_of_yanshen
				duration = 18250
			}
			set_country_flag = feiten_resolved_accord_of_yanshen_peaceably
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_refused_accord_of_yanshen
				duration = 18250
			}
			custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.75.gainAEtt
			hidden_effect = {
				every_known_country = {
					limit = {
						capital_scope = { superregion = yanshen_superregion }
						NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { alliance_with = ROOT }
					}
					add_aggressive_expansion = { who = ROOT value = 25 apply_calc = no }
				}
			}
		}
		add_prestige_excess_to_splendour_effect = { VAL = 20 }
	}

	after = { set_country_flag = feiten_resolved_accord_of_yanshen }
}

	id = flavor_feiten.76

	desc = flavor_feiten.76.desc

		name = flavor_feiten.76.a
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_bombs_over_tianlou_mod
			duration = 1825
		}
		4871 = {
			add_devastation = 50
			add_base_tax = -5
			add_base_production = -5
			add_base_manpower = -5
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = damaged_temple_complex
					duration = -1
				}
				downgrade_temple_wards = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex }
				remove_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = derelict_temple_complex
					duration = -1
				}
				downgrade_temple_wards = yes
			}
		}
		4879 = {
			add_base_tax = 3
			add_base_production = 3
			add_base_manpower = 3
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					R62 = {
						OR = {
							num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
								value = 20
								superregion = yanshen_superregion
							}
							4826 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = feiten_shift_savior_of_yanshen
				country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.77 days = 365 random = 90 }
			}		
			# Yanshen healthy, they more worried about you
			else = {
				set_country_flag = feiten_shift_accord_of_yanshen
				country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.71 days = 365 random = 90 }
				country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.72 days = 730 random = 180 }
				country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.73 days = 1095 random = 270 }
				country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.75 days = 1825 random = 730 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			name = feiten_savior_of_yanshen_scout_balloon_sharing_own
			duration = 3650
		}

				is_in_coalition_war = yes
				war_with = R62
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_savior_of_yanshen_war_balloon_sharing_allies
				duration = 3650
			}
		}

			duration = 3650
		}

				is_in_coalition_war = yes
				war_with = R62
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_savior_of_yanshen_war_balloon_sharing_allies
				duration = 3650
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_savior_of_yanshen_scout_balloon_sharing_allies
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_savior_of_yanshen_scout_balloon_sharing_own
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_savior_of_yanshen_war_balloon_sharing_own
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_yearly_manpower = -4
		add_years_of_income = -1
	}

	# Do nothing
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.78.d
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_coalition_war = yes
				war_with = R62
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = feiten_refused_to_support_allies
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.91
	title = flavor_feiten.91.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.91.desc
	picture = DUTCH_SHIPS_PLUNDERING_eventPicture
	goto = 1430

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { north_ocean_of_the_lost_area = { discover_country = ROOT } } }

	# Try to blast the affected ships out!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.91.a
		add_mil_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 1 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 2 } }
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			# We get all of them out
			1 = { }
			# We lose many of our ships
			1 = {
				add_yearly_sailors = -1
				hidden_effect = {
					multiply_variable = {
						which = feiten_voyage_total_light_ships
						value = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# We have to leave them behind to ensure the survival of our greater fleet
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.91.b
		add_yearly_sailors = -2
		add_prestige = -10
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 0 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 1 } }
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = feiten_voyage_total_light_ships
				value = 0.8
			}
		}
	}

	# A great evacuation with our balloons!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.91.c
		add_mil_power = -100
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 2 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 3 } }
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = feiten_voyage_total_light_ships
				value = 0.8
			}
		}
	}

	after = { hidden_effect = {  country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.92 days = 180 random = 30 } } }
}

			}
		}

			limit = { culture_group = eordan_ruinborn_elf }

				who = ROOT

			}
		}

				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 0 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}

	# Trade dealio
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.92.c
		add_years_of_income = -1
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 1 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 2 } }
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = feiten_voyage_total_light_ships
				value = 0.9
			}
		}
	}

	after = { hidden_effect = {  country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.93 days = 180 random = 30 } } }
}

				every_neighbor_province = { limit = { NOT = { is_sea = yes } } discover_country = ROOT }
			}
			1689 = {
				discover_country = ROOT
				every_neighbor_province = { limit = { NOT = { is_sea = yes } } discover_country = ROOT }
			}
			1683 = {
				discover_country = ROOT
				every_neighbor_province = { limit = { NOT = { is_sea = yes } } discover_country = ROOT }
			}
			1396 = {
				discover_country = ROOT
				every_neighbor_province = { limit = { NOT = { is_sea = yes } } discover_country = ROOT }
			}
		}
		}

	# Murdkather and the Summer Court
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.93.a
		goto = 2037
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 2 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 3 } }
			}
		}
		add_navy_tradition = 10
		set_country_flag = feiten_murdkather_skypost
	}

	# Connect with the Merchant Lords of Sarmadfar
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.93.b
		goto = 2022
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 1 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 2 } }
			}
		}
		define_admiral = {
			fire = 2
			shock = 2
			manuever = 6
			trait = extortioner_personality
			name = "Elanal Sunwake"
		}
		set_country_flag = feiten_bagcatir_skypost
	}

	after = { hidden_effect = {  country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.97 days = 180 random = 30 } } }
}

# We picked the south
# Pirates picking off your flanks
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.94
	title = flavor_feiten.94.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.94.desc
	picture = NAVAL_MILITARY_eventPicture
	goto = 1367

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Sortie out, take no quarter with a show of force!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.94.a
		add_prestige = 10
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					OR = {
						ruler_has_personality = tactical_genius_personality
						ruler_has_personality = navigator_personality
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					mil = 6
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.8
					mil = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.9
					mil = 4
				}
				kill_ruler = yes
			}
			1 = {
				change_mil = 1
				random_list = {
					1 = {
						trigger = { NOT = { ruler_has_max_personalities = yes } NOT = { ruler_has_personality = inspiring_leader_personality } }
						add_ruler_personality = inspiring_leader_personality
					}
					1 = {
						trigger = { NOT = { ruler_has_max_personalities = yes } NOT = { ruler_has_personality = bold_fighter_personality } }
						add_ruler_personality = bold_fighter_personality
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 2 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 3 } }
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = feiten_voyage_total_light_ships
				value = 0.7
			}
		}
	}

	# Jettison cargo from our most vulnerable ships, then defensive positions!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.94.b
		add_years_of_income = -1
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 1 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 2 } }
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = feiten_voyage_total_light_ships
				value = 0.9
			}
		}
	}

	# Proceed as normal
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.94.c
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 0 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 1 } }
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = feiten_voyage_total_light_ships
				value = 0.8
			}
		}
	}

	after = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.95 days = 180 random = 30 } }
}

# Return of the fleet
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.97
	title = flavor_feiten.97.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.97.desc
	picture = AIRSHIP_SKYPORT_eventPicture
	goto = 4879

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# Round the number of ships to nearest down
		# I know there are better ways to do this but w/e
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feiten_voyage_total_light_ships
						value = 1
					}
				}
				subtract_variable = {
					which = feiten_voyage_total_light_ships
					value = 1
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = feiten_voyage_light_ships_left
					value = 1
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = feiten_voyage_total_gold_collected
				which = feiten_voyage_light_ships_left
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = feiten_voyage_total_gold_collected
				value = 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = feiten_voyage_sramaya }
				multiply_variable = {
					which = feiten_voyage_total_gold_collected
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.97.a
		custom_tooltip = feiten_voyage_return_tt
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = feiten_voyage_light_ships_left
					value = 1
				}
			}
			subtract_variable = {
				which = feiten_voyage_light_ships_left
				value = 1
			}
			4879 = { light_ship = ROOT }
			add_treasury = 50
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = feiten_voyage_sramaya_markets }
				add_treasury = 25
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = feiten_voyage_concluded
		set_country_flag = feiten_skyposts_unlocked
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 6 } }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_mythos_of_the_voyage_max
				duration = 36500
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = feiten_voyage_mythos value = 4 } }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_mythos_of_the_voyage_mid
				duration = 36500
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_mythos_of_the_voyage_min
				duration = 36500
			}
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = feiten_the_world_our_oyster_tt
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = feiten_davharral_skypost }
			2913 = { add_province_triggered_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = feiten_murdkather_skypost }
			2037 = { add_province_triggered_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = feiten_bagcatir_skypost }
			2022 = { add_province_triggered_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
		}
	}

	after = {
		clr_country_flag = feiten_davharral_skypost
		clr_country_flag = feiten_murdkather_skypost
		clr_country_flag = feiten_bagcatir_skypost
	}
}

		random_trade_node = {

					NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
				}
				any_trade_node_member_province = {
					owned_by = ROOT

		}

# Build a skyport in an owned province (second one for list refreshes)
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.101
	title = flavor_feiten.100.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.100.desc
	picture = AIRSHIP_SKYPORT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# Pick a bunch of locations
		random_trade_node = {
			limit = {
				all_trade_node_member_province = {
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
				}
				any_trade_node_member_province = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
			}
			random_trade_node_member_province = {
				limit = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag
				save_event_target_as = feitenSkyportTarget1
			}
		}

		random_trade_node = {
			limit = {
				all_trade_node_member_province = {
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
				}
				any_trade_node_member_province = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
			}
			random_trade_node_member_province = {
				limit = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }

				}
				any_trade_node_member_province = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
			}
			random_trade_node_member_province = {
				limit = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag
				save_event_target_as = feitenSkyportTarget10
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Exit
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.back
		every_province = { clr_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
		custom_tooltip = feiten_back_to_skypost_menu_tt
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.100.b
		trigger = { has_saved_event_target = feitenSkyportTarget1 }
		goto = feitenSkyportTarget1

		add_treasury = -1000
		add_dip_power = -50
		event_target:feitenSkyportTarget1 = { add_province_triggered_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
		every_province = { clr_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
	}

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.100.c
		trigger = { has_saved_event_target = feitenSkyportTarget2 }
		goto = feitenSkyportTarget2

# Dismantle a skyport in a province
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.102
	title = flavor_feiten.102.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.102.desc
	picture = AIRSHIP_SKYPORT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget1
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget2
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget3
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget4
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget5
			}
		}
	}

	# Cancel
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.back
		every_province = { clr_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
		custom_tooltip = feiten_back_to_skypost_menu_tt
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.102.b
		trigger = { has_saved_event_target = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget1 }
		goto = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget1

		event_target:feitenDismantleSkyportTarget1 = {
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target
				key = "Skypost Trade Web"
			}
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door_prov
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism_prov
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison_prov
			hidden_effect = {
				event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = feitenActiveSkyports
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_province_flag = clr_skypost
		}
		every_province = { clr_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
	}

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.102.c
		trigger = { has_saved_event_target = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget2 }
		goto = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget2

		event_target:feitenDismantleSkyportTarget2 = { 
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target
				key = "Skypost Trade Web"
			}
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door_prov
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism_prov
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison_prov
			hidden_effect = {
				event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = feitenActiveSkyports
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_province_flag = clr_skypost
		}
		every_province = { clr_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
	}

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.102.d
		trigger = { has_saved_event_target = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget3 }
		goto = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget3

		event_target:feitenDismantleSkyportTarget3 = { 
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target
				key = "Skypost Trade Web"
			}
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door_prov
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism_prov
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison_prov
			hidden_effect = {
				event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = feitenActiveSkyports
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_province_flag = clr_skypost
		}
		every_province = { clr_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
	}

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.102.e
		trigger = { has_saved_event_target = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget4 }
		goto = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget4

		event_target:feitenDismantleSkyportTarget4 = { 
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target
				key = "Skypost Trade Web"
			}
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door_prov
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism_prov
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison_prov
			hidden_effect = {
				event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = feitenActiveSkyports
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_province_flag = clr_skypost
		}
		every_province = { clr_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
	}

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.102.f
		trigger = { has_saved_event_target = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget5 }
		goto = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget5

		event_target:feitenDismantleSkyportTarget5 = { 
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
			remove_trade_modifier = {
				who = event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target
				key = "Skypost Trade Web"
			}
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door_prov
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism_prov
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison_prov
			hidden_effect = {
				event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = feitenActiveSkyports
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_province_flag = clr_skypost
		}
		every_province = { clr_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
	}

	# Refresh list
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.102.g
		country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.103 }
	}

	after = { feiten_update_skypost_trade_modifiers = yes }
}

# Dismantle a skyport in a province (second one for list refreshes)
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.103
	title = flavor_feiten.102.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.102.desc
	picture = AIRSHIP_SKYPORT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget1
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget2
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget3
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget4
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible
					NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target
				save_event_target_as = feitenDismantleSkyportTarget5
			}
		}
	}

	# Cancel
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.back
		every_province = { clr_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
		custom_tooltip = feiten_back_to_skypost_menu_tt
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.102.b

				who = event_target:feiten_or_was_feiten_target

			}
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door_prov
			remove_province_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism_prov

					subtract_variable = {
						which = feitenActiveSkyports
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}

		}
		every_province = { clr_province_flag = feiten_dismantle_skyport_target }
	}

# Skyport menu
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.104
	title = flavor_feiten.104.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.104.desc
	picture = FEITEN_SKYPORT_GUI_PIC_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	# Issue Silken Council Proclamation
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.104.b
		custom_tooltip = silkenProclamationInfoTT
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door }
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationMarketplaceOfIdeas
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism }
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationFeitenFirst
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison }
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationAirliftsAndDefence
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationNone
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.106 } }
		}
	}

	# Construct Skyport
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.104.c
		custom_tooltip = feitenConstructSkypostInfoShortTT
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = feitenSkyportBalance
					value = 1
				}
				any_trade_node = {
					all_trade_node_member_province = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
					}
					any_trade_node_member_province = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.100 }
		}
		# Construct TT
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = cannotConstructSkyportTT
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.105 } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feitenSkyportBalance
						value = 1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = skyportBelowCapTT
			}
			else = { custom_tooltip = skyportNotBelowCapTT }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_trade_node = {
							all_trade_node_member_province = {
								NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
							}
							any_trade_node_member_province = {
								owned_by = ROOT
								province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
								NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = skyportConstructionConditionsNotFulfilledTT
			}
			else = { custom_tooltip = skyportConstructionConditionsFulfilledTT }
		}
	}

	# Dismantle Skyport
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.104.d
		custom_tooltip = feiten_dismantle_skypost_province_tt
		every_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible }
			custom_tooltip = feitenGetNameYellow
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.102 } }
	}

# Second Skyport menu for refreshes
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.105
	title = flavor_feiten.104.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.104.desc
	picture = FEITEN_SKYPORT_GUI_PIC_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	# Issue Silken Council Proclamation
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.104.b
		custom_tooltip = silkenProclamationInfoTT
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door }
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationMarketplaceOfIdeas
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism }
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationFeitenFirst
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison }
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationAirliftsAndDefence
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = activeSilkenProclamationNone
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.106 } }
		}
	}

	# Construct Skyport
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.104.c
		custom_tooltip = feitenConstructSkypostInfoShortTT
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = feitenSkyportBalance
					value = 1
				}
				any_trade_node = {
					all_trade_node_member_province = {
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
					}
					any_trade_node_member_province = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.100 }
		}
		# Construct TT
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = cannotConstructSkyportTT
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = feitenSkyportBalance
						value = 1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = skyportBelowCapTT
			}
			else = { custom_tooltip = skyportNotBelowCapTT }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_trade_node = {
							all_trade_node_member_province = {
								NOT = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
							}
							any_trade_node_member_province = {
								owned_by = ROOT
								province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
								NOT = { has_province_flag = feiten_skyport_target_flag }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = skyportConstructionConditionsNotFulfilledTT
			}
			else = { custom_tooltip = skyportConstructionConditionsFulfilledTT }
		}
	}

	# Dismantle Skyport
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.104.d
		custom_tooltip = feiten_dismantle_skypost_province_tt
		every_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skypost_mod_visible }
			custom_tooltip = feitenGetNameYellow
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.102 } }
	}

# Convene Silken Council
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.106
	title = flavor_feiten.106.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.106.desc
	picture = AIRSHIP_SKYPORT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# the admin one
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.106.a
		change_government_reform_progress = -25
		custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.106.a.tt
		every_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
			custom_tooltip = feitenGetNameYellow
			hidden_effect = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door_prov
					duration = 3650
				}
				add_base_tax = 1
				ROOT = { add_adm_power = -50 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = feitenNewLine
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_silken_proclamation_open_door
			duration = 3650
		}
	}

	# the dip one
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.106.b
		change_government_reform_progress = -25
		custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.106.b.tt
		every_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
			custom_tooltip = feitenGetNameYellow
			hidden_effect = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism_prov
					duration = 3650
				}
				add_base_production = 1
				ROOT = { add_dip_power = -50 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = feitenNewLine
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_silken_proclamation_trade_protectionism
			duration = 3650
		}
		custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.106.b.tt2
	}

	# the mil one
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.106.c
		change_government_reform_progress = -25
		custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.106.c.tt
		every_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = feiten_skyport_handler_mod }
			custom_tooltip = feitenGetNameYellow
			hidden_effect = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison_prov
					duration = 3650
				}
				add_base_manpower = 1
				ROOT = { add_mil_power = -50 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = feitenNewLine
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_silken_proclamation_air_garrison
			duration = 3650
		}
	}

	# NEVERMIND
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.back
		custom_tooltip = feiten_back_to_skypost_menu_tt
	}

	after = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.104 } } }
}

# The old guard of the Silken Council worry
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.110
	title = flavor_feiten.110.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.110.desc
	picture = COUNCIL_TRENT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# We can't risk angering them
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.110.a
		change_statists_vs_orangists = 0.1
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { religion = high_philosophy }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_high_philosophy_assurances
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_silken_council_worries_assuaged
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
	
	# no!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.110.b
		change_statists_vs_orangists = -0.1
		add_papal_influence = 10
		add_republican_tradition_excess_to_mana_effect = { VAL = 5 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_revolt_of_the_silken_turban
			duration = 3650
		}
		4879 = {
			spawn_rebels = {
				size = 3
				type = high_philosophy_rebels
				religion = high_philosophy
			}
			spawn_rebels = {
				size = 3
				type = high_philosophy_rebels
				religion = high_philosophy
			}
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { province_id = 4879 }
				province_group = jellyfish_coast_provinces
			}
			spawn_rebels = {
				size = 2
				type = high_philosophy_rebels
				religion = high_philosophy
			}
			spawn_rebels = {
				size = 2
				type = high_philosophy_rebels
				religion = high_philosophy
			}
		}
	}
}

# A mutiny aboard
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.111
	title = flavor_feiten.111.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.111.desc
	picture = FLAGSHIP_CAPTURED_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Discharge them from service
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.111.a
		add_yearly_sailors = -2
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_discharged_sailors
			duration = 3650
		}
	}

	# Rough them up a bit
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.111.b
		4879 = { add_unrest = 10 }
		add_yearly_manpower = -0.5
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_subdued_sailors
			duration = 3650
		}
	}

	# Send in missionaries among the crews
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.111.c
		add_years_of_income = -2
		random_list = {
			# Success
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					advisor = inquisitor
					has_adm_advisor_3 = yes
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					advisor = inquisitor
					has_adm_advisor_4 = yes
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					advisor = inquisitor
					has_adm_advisor_5 = yes
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = global_missionary_strength
						value = 0.05
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 5
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = global_missionary_strength
						value = 0.1
					}
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = feiten_crew_missionary_success
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
			# Fail
			1 = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = feiten_crew_missionary_rejection
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Flood of foreign missionaries through Cuihoik
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.112
	title = flavor_feiten.112.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.112.desc
	picture = BONFIRE_OF_THE_VANITIES_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Sure let them in
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.112.a
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_ravelian_missionaries
			duration = 7300
		}
		4884 = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_ravelian_society
				duration = -1
			}
			change_religion = ravelian
		}
		change_statists_vs_orangists = -0.1
	}

	# No, they will cause too much trouble
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.112.b
		add_prestige = 10
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		change_statists_vs_orangists = 0.1
	}
}

# Visiting the Ravelian State - who shall we bring to advise us?
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.113
	title = flavor_feiten.113.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.113.desc
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { exists = Z97 }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
				value = 100
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
				value = 100
			}
		}
	}

	# Our Veridical(s)
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.113.a
		trigger = { num_of_cardinals = 1 }
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_church
			loyalty = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
				value = 10
			}
			if = {
				limit = { num_of_cardinals = 3 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { num_of_cardinals = 2 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { invested_papal_influence = 200 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { invested_papal_influence = 100 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 10
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { invested_papal_influence = 50 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 50
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Smaht Shuimu Cadre engineering guy
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.113.b
		trigger = { has_estate = estate_artificers }
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_artificers
			loyalty = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
				value = 10
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_influence = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						influence = 60
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					estate_influence = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						influence = 50
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 15
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					estate_influence = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						influence = 40
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 10
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						estate_influence = {
							estate = estate_artificers
							influence = 40
						}
					}
				}
				subtract_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					estate_loyalty = {
						estate = estate_artificers
						loyalty = 66
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						estate_loyalty = {
							estate = estate_artificers
							loyalty = 33
						}
					}
				}
				subtract_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = -25
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Trust in our ruler
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.113.c
		add_prestige_or_monarch_power = { amount = 10 }
		custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.113_ruler_desc
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { republican_tradition = 99 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { republican_tradition = 95 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 20
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { republican_tradition = 90 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 15
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { republican_tradition = 85 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 10
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { republican_tradition = 80 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 5
				}
			}
			else_if = { limit = { republican_tradition = 60 } }
			else_if = {
				limit = { republican_tradition = 40 }
				subtract_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 10
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { republican_tradition = 20 }
				subtract_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 15
				}
			}
			else = {
				subtract_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 25
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ruler_has_personality = benevolent_personality
						ruler_has_personality = just_personality
						ruler_has_personality = righteous_personality
						ruler_has_personality = kind_hearted_personality
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ruler_has_personality = drunkard_personality
						ruler_has_personality = malevolent_personality
						ruler_has_personality = cruel_personality
					}
				}
				subtract_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationTrustworthiness
					value = 10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { dip = 6 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { dip = 5 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 10
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { dip = 4 }
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { dip = 2 } }
				subtract_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { NOT = { dip = 3 } }
				subtract_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
						export_to_variable = {
							value = trigger_value:adm
							which = rulerAdm
						}
						export_to_variable = {
							value = trigger_value:dip
							which = rulerDip
						}
						export_to_variable = {
							value = trigger_value:mil
							which = rulerMil
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = rulerSkills
							which = rulerAdm
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = rulerSkills
							which = rulerDip
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = rulerSkills
							which = rulerMil
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = rulerSkills
							which = 18
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
						export_to_variable = {
							value = trigger_value:adm
							which = rulerAdm
						}
						export_to_variable = {
							value = trigger_value:dip
							which = rulerDip
						}
						export_to_variable = {
							value = trigger_value:mil
							which = rulerMil
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = rulerSkills
							which = rulerAdm
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = rulerSkills
							which = rulerDip
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = rulerSkills
							which = rulerMil
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = rulerSkills
							which = 15
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 10
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
						export_to_variable = {
							value = trigger_value:adm
							which = rulerAdm
						}
						export_to_variable = {
							value = trigger_value:dip
							which = rulerDip
						}
						export_to_variable = {
							value = trigger_value:mil
							which = rulerMil
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = rulerSkills
							which = rulerAdm
						}

							which = rulerSkills

							which = 12
						}
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = feitenDelegationPersuasiveness
					value = 5
				}

			if = {

						ruler_has_personality = free_thinker_personality

# Colony has a High Philosophy haven 
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.118
	title = flavor_feiten.118.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.118.desc
	picture = ANGLICAN_SERMON_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		any_subject_country = {
			is_colonial_nation_of = ROOT
			liberty_desire = 50
			religion = high_philosophy
			any_owned_province = { religion = high_philosophy }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				is_colonial_nation_of = ROOT
				liberty_desire = 50
				religion = high_philosophy
				any_owned_province = { religion = high_philosophy }
			}
			save_event_target_as = feiten_high_philosophy_fled_country
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { religion = high_philosophy }
				save_event_target_as = feiten_high_philosophy_fled_province
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					development = 10
					religion = high_philosophy
				}
				save_event_target_as = feiten_high_philosophy_fled_province
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					development = 20
					religion = high_philosophy
				}
				save_event_target_as = feiten_high_philosophy_fled_province
			}
		}
	}

	# A heavy hand is needed - intervene directly
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.118.a
		event_target:feiten_high_philosophy_fled_province = {
			change_religion = ravelian
			add_unrest = 5
			add_base_tax = -1
			add_base_manpower = -1
		}
		event_target:feiten_high_philosophy_fled_country = { add_liberty_desire = 10 }
		add_yearly_manpower = -1
	}

	# Concessions, but they need to handle it
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.118.b
		event_target:feiten_high_philosophy_fled_country = {
			add_tariff_value = -0.2
			add_liberty_desire = -20
		}
		event_target:feiten_high_philosophy_fled_province = {
			change_religion = ravelian
			add_unrest = 5
			add_base_tax = -1
			add_base_manpower = -1
		}
		add_dip_power = -100
	}

	# Meh, that is of no worry to us
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.118.c
		event_target:feiten_high_philosophy_fled_country = { add_liberty_desire = -10 }
	}
}

# Colony converts
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.119
	title = flavor_feiten.119.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.119.desc
	picture = JESUTIS_IN_BRAZIL_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		any_subject_country = {
			is_colonial_nation_of = ROOT
			NOT = { religion = ravelian }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				is_colonial_nation_of = ROOT
				NOT = { religion = ravelian }
			}
			save_event_target_as = feiten_converting_colony
		}
	}

	# Lets send missionaries to help em' out
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.119.a
		add_years_of_income = -2
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_colony_ravelian_conversion_parent
			duration = 10950
		}
		event_target:feiten_converting_colony = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = feiten_colony_ravelian_conversion_colony
				duration = 10950
			}
			change_religion = ravelian
			capital_scope = {
				area = {
					change_religion = ravelian
				}
			}
			add_liberty_desire = -10
		}
		add_papal_influence = 10
	}

	# They can handle it on their own, but cool!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.119.b
		event_target:feiten_converting_colony = {
			change_religion = ravelian
			capital_scope = { change_religion = ravelian }
		}
	}
}

# Lightning Jellyfish event
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.202
	title = flavor_feiten.202.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.202.desc
	picture = AIRSHIP_SKYPORT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Let 'er rip
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.202.a
		add_mil_power = -50
		random_hired_mercenary_company = {
			limit = { template = merc_feiten_lightning_jellyfish }
			location = {
				if = {
					limit = { controller = { war_with = ROOT } }
					change_controller = ROOT
					add_devastation = 50
					random_list = {
						1 = { add_base_production = -1 }
						1 = { add_base_tax = -1 }
						1 = { add_base_manpower = -1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Nevermind
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.202.b
		highlight = yes
	}
}

# Start research - who shall lead our efforts?
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.210
	title = flavor_feiten.210.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.210.desc
	picture = GENERALS_DISCUSSING_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}

	# Our own Shuimu + House of Fire and Water
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.210.a
		add_estate_artificers_loyalty_effect = yes
		add_adm_power = -100
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				# Great success
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						university = 20
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						cathedral = 20
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						check_variable = {
							which = feiten_number_of_shuimu_engineering_cadre_facilities_investments
							value = 20
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						check_variable = {
							which = feiten_number_of_shuimu_engineering_cadre_facilities_investments
							value = 15
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						check_variable = {
							which = feiten_number_of_shuimu_engineering_cadre_facilities_investments
							value = 10
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						innovativeness = 99
					}
					change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 2 }
				}
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 0 } }
			}
		}
	}

	# The scholars of Yangcheng
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.210.b
		if = {
			limit = { 4861 = { owned_by = ROOT } }
			4861 = { add_local_autonomy = 100 }
			add_adm_power = -50
		}
		else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = { owns = 4861 }
				add_trust = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 25
					mutual = yes
				}
				add_favors = {
					who = ROOT
					amount = 10
				}
			}
			add_dip_power = -50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 3 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}

	# Call in some favours from gnomish allies
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.210.c
		trigger = { any_ally = { culture_group = gnomish } }
		add_dip_power = -100
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				culture_group = gnomish
				alliance_with = ROOT
			}
			add_trust = {
				who = ROOT
				value = 25
				mutual = yes
			}
			add_favors = {
				who = ROOT
				amount = 10
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 2 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}

	# Leverage Ravelian community at large
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.210.d
		trigger = { religion = ravelian }
		add_papal_influence = -50
		add_curia_treasury = 1000
		add_treasury = -1000

			random_list = {
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						calc_true_if = {
							amount = 20
							all_country = { religion = ravelian }
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						calc_true_if = {
							amount = 10
							all_country = { religion = ravelian }
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						calc_true_if = {
							amount = 5
							all_country = { religion = ravelian }
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 5
						num_of_cardinals = 3
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						num_of_cardinals = 2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						num_of_cardinals = 1
					}
					change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 2 }
				}
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}

	after = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.211 days = 730 random = 180  } } }
}

# Which option to pursue?
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.211
	title = flavor_feiten.211.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.211.desc
	picture = NEO_CONFUCIANISM_INCIDENT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Vitriol + Iron -> Hydrogen Gas [Fe(s) + H2SO4(aq) -> H2(g) + FeSO4(aq)]: Low tech
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.211.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = MaxArtificePoints
					value = 100
				}
			}
			add_mil_power = -50
			add_years_of_income = -0.5
			debuff_artifice_points_5 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = MaxArtificePoints
					value = 50
				}
			}
			add_mil_power = -100
			add_years_of_income = -1
			debuff_artifice_points_5 = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_mil_power = -200
			add_years_of_income = -2
			debuff_artifice_points_5 = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 1 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 0 } }
			}
		}
	}

	# Electrolysis of water [2 H2O(l) -> 2 H2(g) + O2(g)]: Mid tech
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.211.a
		trigger = { has_estate = estate_mages }
		if = {
			limit = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_mages
					influence = 66
				}
			}
			add_adm_power = -50
			add_years_of_income = -0.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_mages
					influence = 33
				}
			}
			add_adm_power = -100
			add_years_of_income = -1
		}
		else = {
			add_adm_power = -200
			add_years_of_income = -2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 2 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}

	# From coal gasification: High tech
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.211.c
		trigger = { coal = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
					value = 3
					trade_goods = coal
					has_building = university
					has_production_building_trigger = yes
					has_manufactory_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			add_adm_power = -100
			add_years_of_income = -1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
					value = 2
					trade_goods = coal
					has_building = university
					has_production_building_trigger = yes
					has_manufactory_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			add_adm_power = -200
			add_years_of_income = -2
		}
		else = {
			add_adm_power = -400
			add_years_of_income = -4
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { trade_goods = coal }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = feiten_coal_gasification
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 2 } }
				1 = { change_variable = { which = feiten_lighter_than_air_tracker value = 3 } }
			}
		}
	}

	after = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.212 days = 730 random = 180  } } }
}

	desc = flavor_feiten.220.desc
