		name = flavor_feiten.220.a
		trigger = {
			any_known_country = {
				any_owned_province = { trade_goods = mithril }
				has_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 150
				}
			}
		}
		add_treasury = -100000
		if = {
			limit = { 4885 = { owned_by = ROOT } }
			4885 = { change_trade_goods = mithril }
		}
		else = { random_owned_province = { change_trade_goods = mithril } }
	}

	# Preferential treatment for that country's traders
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.220.b
		trigger = {
			any_known_country = {
				any_owned_province = { trade_goods = mithril }
				has_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 150
				}
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_province = { trade_goods = mithril }
				has_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 150
				}
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { trade_goods = mithril }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_mithril_trade_deal_ally
					duration = 7300
				}
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_mithril_trade_deal_own
			duration = 7300
		}
	}

	# Grease the wheels with some money, bring in merchants/eunuchs to oversee
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.220.c
		trigger = { any_owned_province = { trade_goods = mithril } }
		add_years_of_income = -5
		add_estate_burghers_loyalty_effect = yes
		add_estate_eunuchs_anb_loyalty_effect = yes
	}

	# Let's bring in our military to oversee and use as labour
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.220.d
		trigger = { any_owned_province = { trade_goods = mithril } }
		add_yearly_manpower = -2.5
		add_yearly_sailors = -2.5
		add_estate_artificers_loyalty_effect = yes
	}

	after = { country_event = { id = flavor_feiten.221 days = 730 random = 180 } }
}

country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.232
	title = flavor_feiten.232.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.232.desc
	picture = USA_TEA_PARTY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.232.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = feiten_of_pistons_and_flames_envoy }
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:feiten_of_pistons_and_flames_owner_province = {
						has_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							value = 150
						}
						has_spy_network_from = {
							who = ROOT
							value = 75
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = flavor_feiten.232.partnershiptt

# Ending Event
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.233
	title = flavor_feiten.233.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.233.desc
	picture = ATMOSPHERIC_ENGINE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Kewl kewl
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.233.a
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_flag
			feiten_of_pistons_and_flames_railroads = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = feiten_the_steam_engine_railroads
					duration = 7300
				}
			}
			feiten_of_pistons_and_flames_ironclads = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = feiten_the_steam_engine_ironclads
					duration = 7300
				}
			}
			feiten_of_pistons_and_flames_factories = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = feiten_the_steam_engine_factories
					duration = 7300
				}
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_of_pistons_and_steam_mod
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = feiten_of_pistons_and_flames_railroads
			clr_country_flag = feiten_of_pistons_and_flames_ironclads
			clr_country_flag = feiten_of_pistons_and_flames_factories
			clr_country_flag = feiten_of_pistons_and_flames_bribed
			clr_country_flag = feiten_of_pistons_and_flames_envoy
		}
	}
}

# Upgrade Grand Skyport no DLC
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.270
	title = flavor_feiten.270.title
	desc = flavor_feiten.270.desc
	picture = AIRSHIP_SKYPORT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.270.a
		if = {
			limit = { 4879 = { has_province_modifier = feiten_grand_skyport_level_1 } }
			4879 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_grand_skyport_level_2
					duration = -1
				}
				remove_province_modifier = feiten_grand_skyport_level_1
			}
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_artificers loyalty = 10 }
			mission_reward_artifice_points_3 = yes
			custom_tooltip = updateGrandSkyportTT
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 4879 = { has_province_modifier = feiten_grand_skyport_level_2 } }
			4879 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_grand_skyport_level_3
					duration = -1
				}
				remove_province_modifier = feiten_grand_skyport_level_2
			}
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_artificers loyalty = 10 }
			mission_reward_artifice_points_5 = yes
			custom_tooltip = updateGrandSkyportBeegTT
		}
		else = {
			4879 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = feiten_grand_skyport_level_1
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_artificers loyalty = 5 }
			mission_reward_artifice_points_1 = yes
			custom_tooltip = updateGrandSkyportTT
		}
	}
}

# Traditional tea cultivation vs "new" crops and shit from Aelantir
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.300
	title = flavor_feiten.300.t
	desc = flavor_feiten.300.desc
	picture = TRADE_GOODS_PLANTATION_GOODS_IN_WAREHOUSE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# Cocoa province
		random_province = {
			limit = {
				country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT
				trade_goods = tea
				area = hungngon_area
			}
			save_event_target_as = cocoa_province_target
		}
		# Sweet potatoes province
		random_province = {
			limit = {
				country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT
				trade_goods = tea
				OR = {
					area = wanglam_area
					area = jyutsai_area
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = sweet_potatoes_province_target
		}
	}

	# Nah dog
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.300.a
		add_estate_burghers_loyalty_effect = yes
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_embrace_traditional_crops
			duration = 7300
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = {
				which = feiten_schism_balance
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

	# Embrace it!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.300.b
		add_republican_tradition = -5
		add_prestige = -10
		if = {
			limit = { has_saved_event_target = cocoa_province_target }
			event_target:cocoa_province_target = {
				change_trade_goods = cocoa
				add_base_production = 2
				add_base_tax = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_saved_event_target = sweet_potatoes_province_target }
			event_target:sweet_potatoes_province_target = {
				change_trade_goods = grain
				add_base_production = 2
				add_base_tax = 2
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = feiten_embracing_new_world_crops
			duration = 7300
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = feiten_schism_balance
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Questions about excessive Gommo influence arises
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.301
	title = flavor_feiten.301.t
	desc = flavor_feiten.301.desc
	picture = ACCUSATION_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# And we should all follow their example
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.301.a
		small_increase_of_gnomish_tolerance_effect = yes
		add_republican_tradition = -10
		change_innovativeness = 5
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_artificers
			loyalty = -10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = feiten_schism_balance
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

	# We must all be wary of insidious foreign influences - sieze their estates!
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.301.b
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_burghers
			loyalty = -10
		}
		medium_decrease_of_gnomish_tolerance_effect = yes
		add_years_of_income = 0.5
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_any_gnomish_pop_trigger = yes }
			add_unrest = 5
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_any_gnomish_pop_trigger = yes }
			spawn_rebels = {
				type = noble_rebels
				size = 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = {
				which = feiten_schism_balance
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Silken Council arguement boils over
country_event = {
	id = flavor_feiten.302
	title = flavor_feiten.302.t
	desc = flavor_feiten.302.desc
	picture = BURGHER_ESTATE_UPSET_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Support the Old Guard
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.302.a
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = {
				which = feiten_schism_balance
				value = 1
			}
		}
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
	}

	# Support the Reformists
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.302.b
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = feiten_schism_balance
				value = 1
			}
		}
		change_innovativeness = 5
	}

	# Mediate between the two
	option = {
		name = flavor_feiten.302.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = feiten_schism_balance
				value = 0
			}
		}
		add_dip_power = -50
		random_list = {
			# Mediation is succesful
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					dip = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					dip = 6
				}
				add_republican_tradition_excess_to_mana_effect = { VAL = 10 }
			}
			# Mediation fails
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					dip = 1
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					dip = 2
				}
				add_republican_tradition = -5
				reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
			}
		}
	}
}
